Changzhou 66

Handover of Salaries for Staff of the Public Property Office: The term of office of Tu Xiaohuan, the former director of the Wuyi Public Property Office, had expired, and the County Government reappointed Zhou Jiping as the director, Lin Junbao as the deputy director, and Wu Jun, He Naiyang, Bao Zongming, and Wu Jiguang as accountants. The new and old directors carried out the handover at the office at 4:00 PM on the 11th. They counted and received 4,669 yuan in cash on hand. The remaining items will be jointly calculated clearly.

Resumption of Work by Carpenters: Wuyi carpenters went on strike on the 10th due to a labor dispute over wage increases. After negotiations between the two parties that evening, a solution was reached after much debate. The mediator worked hard to persuade them to resume work uniformly on the 11th to avoid further losses to the workers. As for the issue of wages, the workers' representatives Zhang Fusheng and others went to the county to request a fair judgment as soon as possible.

Additional Probationary Judge Appointed to the County Court: The Jiangsu Higher Court, due to the large backlog of civil and criminal cases in the Wujin County Court, specially appointed Li Wenwei to come to Changzhou as a probationary judge, with a deadline of two months to clear the backlog of civil and criminal cases.

Zhenjiang 67

Chamber of Commerce Organizes a Pledge to Use Domestic Goods: The Zhenjiang County Chamber of Commerce Reorganization Committee, believing that rising commodity prices and inflationary pressures harm both national economy and the people's livelihood, organized a National Products Movement Conference and prepared display cabinets to showcase domestic goods, so that the public can know that domestic goods are not necessarily inferior to foreign goods. Merely chanting slogans without leading by example will not only make it difficult to achieve the effect of resistance, but also easily invite ridicule from foreigners. Therefore, on the 13th and 14th of this month, lectures will be held at the County Party Headquarters, and on the 15th and 16th, lectures will be held at the Boxian Gongyuan. Pledges will be requested to permanently use domestic goods. The pledge is as follows: "I swear to use domestic goods with sincerity, promote domestic goods, and resolve to remain steadfast and unwavering forever. If my words and actions do not match, may I be abandoned by the people of the country."

The Organization of Fishermen's Associations Should Follow a Defined Procedure: The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Agriculture and Mining investigated the Fishermen's Association Law, which was previously promulgated by the National Government to take effect on July 1st. The case has now been communicated for compliance. Now that the date of implementation is approaching, in addition to the rules for the implementation of the law being submitted for review and then promulgated by the ministry, the organization of all fishermen's associations should follow the legal procedure, with the establishment of the county fishermen's association first, followed by the establishment of the fishermen's association federation. One uses natural persons as organizational members, and the other uses legal persons as organizational members. The two are completely different. The regulations are very clear and should be communicated to all places for consistent compliance to clarify the procedure and emphasize the law.

Yangzhou 68

Pawning Rags to Maintain Security: Most of the sojourning residents in Yangzhou are former subordinates of the Sun and Ma armies. During this time, wounded soldiers came to Yangzhou. Some of the unscrupulous sojourning residents would often take advantage of the situation, leading to undesirable acts. On the afternoon of the 10th, someone even brought a bundle of rags to the Dunjidian pawnshop, pretending to pawn them for tens of yuan. The pawnshop gave him two yuan, but he angrily threw them away. On the 11th, the pawnshop did not dare to open for business. Other pawnshops were also wary. The county government, therefore, held a meeting to discuss maintaining security. As a result, additional police officers and merchant corps members were assigned to each city gate and sent to the 92 districts to protect the police teams responsible for loaning disaster relief funds (disaster relief funds will be distributed starting from the 10th and can be completed by the evening of the 12th, then additional personnel will be assigned). At the same time, Ge Zheng, the director of the Public Security Bureau, sent officers to investigate secretly. Upon encountering suspicious activity, they should report to the police, who will be dispatched by the county to coordinate with the military and police to handle the matter, in order to avoid negligence.

The Dog's Tail in the Collapsing River Saves Lives: Regarding the case of the sinking of the Pujilun passenger ship in the area of ​​Jiaxingqiao Liuxi, Zhou Yefu, an employee of the motor company, mentioned that there was a large black dog that stayed by the collapsing river all day long. It suddenly disappeared three days before the collapse. When the collapse was about to occur, the dog suddenly reappeared, lying down for a moment. When the ship reached the river and collapsed, the dog also entered the water and swam ashore. Its tail was held by a person who was able to survive. It was found to be a Wang from the east乡. This is also a strange event.

Nantong 69

Water and Land Police Teams Jointly Suppress Bandits: Recently, a large group of bandits has gathered at the border between Nantong and Haimen counties, causing great harm. The provincial government, based on the reports from the two county magistrates of Tonghai, dispatched water and land provincial police teams and two shallow-water warships to jointly block and suppress them. Li Changjiang, the commander of the provincial police team, arrived in Tongzhou on the 11th to supervise the team's suppression.

Establishment of Market Police in Various Markets in Tongtai: In the areas west of the Fan Gong Dike in the Tongtai region of Huainan, the duties of anti-smuggling and arresting thieves are handled by the anti-smuggling camp. The area east of the dike is very large. The various markets in the two regions are jointly establishing market police. The necessary expenses are collected from the barrel price. It has been decided to be jointly managed by officials and merchants. Two major police teams will be temporarily established. One major team headquarters will be set up in Nantong and one in Dongtai. The establishment has been approved by the Salt Administration of the Ministry of Finance.

Comforting and Recruiting Refugees in the Eastern Districts: Since the bandit riots last autumn in the eastern districts of Tongyi, the wealthy households have fled. Recently, the bandit forces have gradually subsided, and the administrative organs have been reorganized. Those who fled are being persuaded to return to their villages. Those who were coerced into becoming bandits are allowed to rehabilitate themselves and be exempted from investigation. Water and land transportation will be repaired and restored to its original condition in the shortest possible time. The provincial and county police teams stationed in the territory are deeply concerned about the remaining bandits fleeing and are implementing daily patrols.

Pinghu 70

Stray Bullet Wounds a Cow's Back: At about 2:00 PM yesterday, seven private salt boats were passing through Dongnantang, Guan Chu Village, when they encountered three business-managed anti-smuggling patrol boats. The two sides opened fire for about ten minutes. The anti-smuggling force was weak, and two patrol officers were injured. One salt boat was captured. At that time, the farmers were working in the fields and were extremely panicked. Stray bullets rained down. Although no one was injured, a cow belonging to the Ma family had a hole in its back and is currently being treated.

The Gold Ring Was Snatched and Recovered: The old servant of Hu Jiufang in the back of the county was organizing laundry in front of the door the night before last when the gold ring on her ear was suddenly snatched by a bandit. The servant shouted loudly, and Xiao Si, who was shaking a boat, and a cake seller who lived nearby gave chase. They managed to recover both the person and the stolen goods.

Hangzhou 71

Accused Criminals to Be Escorted to the Province for Scheduled Interrogation: At the time of the Zhuji peasant army riots, the provincial government immediately dispatched the Third Security Regiment to suppress the revolt upon receiving the report. After arriving, the regiment captured seven key criminals and escorted them to the province for temporary detention in the Army Prison. It is understood that the provincial government considers the details obtained from the two trials to be serious. It is rumored that the government has scheduled the 16th to bring forth the criminals for a secret trial.

Regulations for Compensation and Relocation Prices: The Hangzhou-Jiang Railway Bureau has begun to acquire land for the Xiao-Chang Railway and has specially stipulated compensation prices for land, attachments, and relocation, divided into five categories: (1) Houses, (2) Crops, (3) Trees, (4) Tombs, (5) Memorial Arches. The bureau has submitted them to the Department of Construction and issued a notice to the county magistrates along the route yesterday (12th) to comply with them.

Shortage of Grain in Wenzhou Area: The Zhejiang Provincial Government received a telegram from Fang Guanying and others, citizens of Yongjia, stating that Wenzhou is suffering from drought, and the displaced are everywhere. Bandit police incidents are frequent, and people's livelihoods are extremely difficult. There is a shortage of grain, and people are panicking about food. They requested the county to quickly allocate funds to control prices and provide relief in order to save lives. The government has ordered the Relief Committee to investigate.

Ningbo 72

Two Robbery Cases in Broad Daylight: (1) Zhou Xingsheng, an apprentice at the Yuanlixiang Kerosene Store in Cuiyaqian, this city, held 18 payment orders yesterday (10th) morning, totaling more than 2,000 yuan in silver, to register the dates at the Shunda Store in Jiangdong. Unexpectedly, on his way back, he was robbed by a bandit on the old Jiang Bridge, and the entire package of payment orders was snatched and fled. The police were immediately notified to pursue the bandit. Fan Qihua and other officers from the post there chased the bandit to the Xinyuanji gate at the entrance of Jiangdong Gray Street, where they caught him and found the stolen goods. The bandit confessed his name as Xin Xiaogou, a native of this county who lives in Taogong Mountain and makes a living by fishing. He admitted to robbing the package of payment orders. The director of the office immediately presented the bandit to the City Public Security Bureau for interrogation. (2) Five bandits suddenly arrived near Zhonggong Temple, Jiangdong, this city, at about 5:00 PM yesterday (10th), each holding a pistol. They robbed seven stores in a row, including Liang Shaoji Rice Store, Jishun Cotton Store, and Sanyangtai Native Goods Store, for a loss of more than 500 yuan. After obtaining the stolen goods, the bandits fled towards Shitou Road. Villagers rang the bell to gather a crowd to encircle them. Near Zhou Shuidu, they captured four bandits: Wang Abao, Zhou Shao, Xu Zhaohai, and Wang Agan. The third team of the patrol team stationed at Lingxian Temple temporarily detained them and scheduled them to be sent to the City Public Security Bureau for interrogation today.

Scheduled Repair of the Xinjian Bridge: The Xinjian Bridge Management Office decided to repair the bridgehead of the Xinjian Bridge from the 20th to the 23rd of this month. At that time, traffic will be stopped and replaced by boats for pedestrians. However, in case of rain, the repair will have to be postponed.

Customs Burns Confiscated Opium: The Zhejiang Customs Taxation Department burned the opium confiscated from April 1st of this year to the end of last month at the customs gate at about 10:00 AM yesterday (10th). A total of 204 taels of Sichuan opium and 52 taels of fake opium were burned. Many people, including Zuo Jian of the County Party Headquarters, Mao Zhongdan, the supervisor of the Customs Supervisory Office, and representatives from the court and public security bureau, were present to supervise. Because this batch of opium was relatively small, lime water was mixed with the opium and poured into the river to save time.

Shangyu 73

Public Criticism of Unburned Opium: During the June 3rd commemoration of Lin Zexu's 90th anniversary of opium prohibition, the county government publicly burned more than 50 opium pipes, lamps, and trays in the Yimiao Temple. Local public opinion has been expressing dissatisfaction that the county government, according to the report of Shen Xianheng, the acting director of the Baiguan Public Security Branch Bureau, seized a female trafficker named Fan Lu in a Caojiang boat on December 5th of last year and seized 60 taels of opium. This opium is still stored in the accounting office and was not burned on that day.

Communist Zhen Yuqing and Others Executed in Shanghai: Zhen Yuqing, a native of Gaotabu, North Gate Street, in the city, was 37 years old and worked for a coal company in the French Concession of Shanghai. In May, he and his fellow villager, Pan Atang, a coppersmith, were arrested in Shanghai for participating in a secret Communist Party meeting. At the same time, about 100 people were arrested. After interrogation by the military and political authorities, it was reported that a total of more than 30 people were sentenced to death. Zhen and Pan were among them and were executed by firing squad in Longhua earlier this month. Zhen's family still has four people in his original hometown: his parents, wife, and younger brother. His father, Laiyou, and younger brother, Fuqing, are all farmers who support themselves. An elder sister works as a servant in Shanghai. Pan is the cousin of Pan Axing, who runs the Pan Juxing Copper Shop at Xinjiekou in this city. His father is deceased, and his mother is alive. Both families are extremely poor. Since receiving the news of their deaths, their parents have been grief-stricken and are critically ill in bed.

Hefei 74

The Fifth District Organizes a Patrol Team to Defend Against Bandits: More than a thousand bandits have recently been discovered in the area of Sanjuesi Town, which borders Hefeiliu and three counties of Shou. They are carrying out robberies and kidnappings. The residents are fleeing. County Magistrate Wang plans to join forces with the Third Detachment after they arrive in Hefei to suppress the bandits. However, all sectors of the city are concerned about the tense city defense and have repeatedly held meetings to decide to organize a patrol team of the five districts in the city. Each district will send fifty people to patrol day and night to assist the military and police. The team was formed on the 7th.

Dispute Over the Change of Director of the Changlin Public Security Bureau: After Wang Xianxing, the director of the Changlinhe Public Security Bureau, was accused and removed from office, the County Government appointed Zhang Qi, the former director of the Changlinhe Public Security Bureau, as acting director. The Civil Affairs Office appointed Wu Jian to go to Changlin to take over. However, because Zhang had a good relationship with the local community, various businesses vowed to keep him, sending public telegrams to the Civil Affairs Office requesting the revocation of the order and refusing the new appointment. Wu was in a dilemma and also telegraphed the province for instructions.

Letters

Letter from Wu Zhikun of Fengxian 75

(Omitted above) I respectfully acknowledge receipt of your newspaper's reporter's letter. I, Wu Zhikun, hired Dr. Wang Jielin on March 25th of this year to treat my hemorrhoids. Due to the strong effect of the medicine, I suffered severe pain for ten days and was in frequent danger. Later, I mistakenly used the raw materials of the Western medicine iodine formula, resulting in complete swelling and rotting of my anus. For several months now, not only has the fistula not been removed, but I have also been unable to leave my house for even half a step. I am suffering both physically and financially. At the same time, my old friend Qu Jun Hongda also heard that he was misled by Dr. Wang (this fact will be published in the New Pudong Newspaper). I believe that incompetent doctors recklessly use medications, treating patients' lives as child's play, and are truly harmful to society. Therefore, I entrusted your newspaper reporter to express this, so that those who hear it will know to be wary. I have specially prepared this letter to testify. I do not know if Dr. Wang searches his heart in the dead of night and feels any guilt. Please publish it in the "Letters to the Editor" column to show the truth. I respectfully wish you peace. Wu Zhikun of Fengxian respectfully inquires, July 3rd.

Letter from the Fengxian County Chinese Medicine Association 76

We respectfully inform you that according to the report of Wang Jielin, a member of the Sixth Branch of our association, he was quite surprised to see a report in the newspaper about a member's malpractice causing death. The reason is that Qu Hongkui was suffering from a boil. He first sought treatment from Dr. Zhang Yunjie in the same town and then invited our member to treat him. The situation was already thorny (word as in the original text). Later, several doctors were consulted for treatment, but none were effective. After a week, he went to Shilong Hospital in Shanghai for treatment, which was ineffective, and he died the next day. This matter has nothing to do with our member. Also, Wu Zhikun, the section chief of the Finance Bureau, suffered from hemorrhoids. Introduced by Wang Xizhang, the judicial clerk of the county government, he was repeatedly treated in Nanyi in March of last spring and has recovered. There were no accidents. Why is this matter reported in the New Shen and New Pudong newspapers? It is very hateful. After investigation, it was found that non-members intentionally fabricated this. It is likely that the reporter heard false rumors. Therefore, we specially request your association to make a factual statement so that the truth will be revealed in the future, which is for the public good. Based on this, after investigation, it was found that Qu Hongkui died of boils because he was not careful about what he ate, and the toxin exploded. Several doctors were consulted for treatment, but there was no way to save him. It has nothing to do with Dr. Wang. Previously, we read a news item in the "Correspondence" column of your newspaper about a malpractice in Fengxian causing death, which does not conform to the facts. Our association has the responsibility to protect the reputation of doctors and should send personnel to investigate the illegal individuals who spread rumors so that they can be prosecuted. In addition to issuing separate letters, we are corresponding and requesting that your newspaper publish the facts in the "Letters to the Editor" column to clarify the public matter. Yang Kuisheng, Cao Xincong, and Xiao Diping, standing committee members of the Fengxian County Chinese Medicine Association.

Sports 77

The Chinese Tennis Team Wins All Matches Yesterday Against Meiji

Lin, Qiu, and Jiang Show Great Skill

Lin Baohua and Jiang Daozhang Win Two Singles Matches; Qiu and Lin Win One Doubles Match

The University Team Loses... Only Wins One Doubles Match

Today, Meiji Plays Against the Japanese Team; Tomorrow, They Play Against Portugal

(1) Welcoming the Meiji Delegation to Shanghai 78

The Meiji University tennis team from Japan, a group of eight, arrived at Wusong around 9 AM yesterday aboard the Toyama Maru. They then took a small ferry to the Wayside Wharf. Those who came to welcome them included Mr. Hao Boyang, Mr. Lin Baohua, Mr. Xu Zhendong, Mr. Uchida and Mr. Kimura of the Japanese Tennis Club, and representatives of the Meiji University Shanghai Alumni Association, Mr. Maruyama and Mr. Yama. After disembarking, they went directly to the Mitsubishi Club on Route Lafayette (present-day Fuxing Road) to stay. They played their first match against the China and University teams yesterday, with good results. Today at 3 PM, they will compete against the Japanese residents.

(2) China Achieves Complete Victory Over Meiji 79

The match between Meiji and the Chinese team, with two singles and one doubles match, was a best-of-five-sets format. It started at 3:30 PM. The final doubles match started too late and was changed to a best-of-three-sets format. In the end, China achieved a complete victory. The match results are as follows:

Singles...Both Matches Won 80

Lin Baohua defeats Otakura. Lin Baohua was initially at a disadvantage in the first set. He excels at placement, but his shots lacked power, allowing his opponent to capitalize and lose two consecutive games. In the third and fifth games, he seized victory, slightly turning the tide to 2-3. Unexpectedly, the floodgates opened, and the momentum shifted entirely. Otakura consistently executed effective forehand and backhand shots, gradually gaining the upper hand. Soon, Lin lost the first set with a score of 2-6. In the second set, Lin was confident and his arm was powerful. His shots were like arrows, doing exactly what he wanted. Otakura was panic-stricken and at a loss, entirely under Lin's control and losing decisively 0-6. From the third set onwards, Lin was well aware that his opponent's weakness was his weak backhand. Eight or nine times out of ten, he placed the ball there, and he won easily. He was slightly careless in the sixth game, allowing his opponent to win. Lin still won the third set 6-1. After a short break, the intense battle resumed. Otakura was spirited, with great energy, alternating left and right hits, swift and powerful. Lin was troubled and lost two consecutive games. Lin regained his composure and regained the advantage. In the end, Lin won the fourth set 6-4, securing the victory. Umpire: Xu Zhendong.

Jiang Daozhang defeats Okamoto. The two men were physically strong and their postures and attitudes resembled brothers. The techniques they demonstrated in the game appeared to come from the same source. Okamoto was fierce and won four consecutive games. Jiang won back the fifth game, then lost the sixth, resulting in a 1-5 disadvantage. The hundreds of spectators were disappointed. Jiang was steady and composed, and he continued to improve. He first made a strong effort to advance, then created a tie, and ultimately won the first set 7-5. The situation was similar in the second set with the two players closely following each other. Both men were extremely powerful, leading to many wild balls. Okamoto's serves were often mishandled, often failing to clear the net, resulting in his own undoing and loss of points.

A group photo of the China, Meiji and University teams (photographed by Wang Kai)

The number of these errors were quite high. Jiang was behind at 5-5 and then won 7-5. This was due to this reason. The two men took turns winning each game in the third set, with each winning two games at a time. Jiang went first, followed by Okamoto, then Jiang again, and then Okamoto reaching 4-4. Jiang then added two consecutive games, winning the set 6-4.

The total score was three wins to zero. Umpire: Ma Detai.

Doubles... One Match Also Won 81

Lin Baohua and Qiu Feihai defeat Matsuo and Sagara. Qiu served well, succeeding on his first try, and won two consecutive games. Judging by the overall situation, the skills of Matsuo and Sagara are not as good as those of Lin and Qiu. However, they made relentless efforts to win, and took advantage of the confusion of Lin and Qiu to win back two games. From then on, the teams were closely matched and Lin and Qiu were unable to maintain their advantage. Unexpectedly, after 6-6, the Japanese went on the offensive and won the first set 8-6, earning the audience's applause and praise. In the second set, Lin and Qiu stepped up their efforts. Their hearts and minds were in sync and these renowned players proved to be in a different class. They soon won the second set 6-3. When the third set began, the sun was setting and dusk was approaching. Sagara's serves were good, and their performance was slightly improved, but their resolve was shaky with mistakes. In the end they couldn't match the composure of the two veteran Lin and Qiu. As a result, Lin and Qiu won again 6-4. At that time, the land was vast and the ball shadows were blurred. The intense match came to an end. Umpire: Hao Boyang.

(3) Meiji Defeats the University Team 82

Meiji wins two singles matches and one doubles match.

The University team wins only one doubles match.

Meiji played against the Shanghai Universities mixed team in two singles and two doubles matches, using a best-of-three-sets format to determine the winners. The matches also started at 3:30 PM. In the end, the University team only won one doubles match, with Wang Minshi and Zheng Tuikai winning, while all other matches were lost. The situation is recorded below:

Singles Two Matches... University Team Loses All 83

Komatsu defeats Zheng Zhaojia. The two men both favored topspin shots. Zheng Zhaojia made aggressive advances and was able to respond effectively, but Komatsu was equally strong, fighting back and creating a fierce battle. The scores were very even, making it difficult to see who was superior. Later, Zheng used a powerful serve to defeat his opponent and win the first set 7-5. The situation was the same from the second set, with the two men retreated and hit groundstrokes from the baseline, with very few net plays. As a result, Komatsu also won the set 7-5, making the score 1-1. The third set became the focus of the victory. Both sides were cautious, worked hard on offense, and the game reached 4-4. Observing Zheng's ball momentum, there was a good chance of winning, but he lost too many points, leading to a loss. Komatsu also won the third set 6-4, making the score 2-1. Umpire: Detta.

Seo defeats Chen Guocheng. Chen Guocheng is a rising star in the Shanghai tennis world, and his tennis skills are also remarkable, especially his topspin shots. Seo, however, had deeply rooted skills and was very steady. Under the back-and-forth, Chen looked inadequate. He lost the first set 1-6. Chen improved slightly from the second set, but the score was still lower and difficult to surpass Seo. As a result, Seo won the second set 6-4. Umpire: Hu Xiansheng.

Doubles... Each Team Wins One Match 84

Otakura (big) and Otakura (small) defeat Hu Qifeng and Hu Qizhuo.

The doubles match between the Otakura brothers and the Hu brothers began at 5:30 PM. The Otakura brothers were well-coordinated, with great communication, able to respond effectively, and handled the game with a calm attitude. Hu Qifeng and Hu Qizhuo, though well-trained, were one step behind, and were flustered. As a result, the Otakura brothers won 2-0, with scores of 6-0 and 6-3. Umpire: Zhou Jiaqi. The match only lasted for a short while.

Zheng Tuikai and Wang Minshi defeat Seo and Mike.

Of all the matches yesterday, only Zheng Tuikai and Wang Minshi won a doubles match, saving face. However, watching Zheng and Wang's score of 1-6 in the first set, their victory looked to be hanging by a thread. However, they were able to persevere and were not flustered at all, and eventually reversed the defeat, which was no easy feat. After the start of the game, Wang and Zheng’s attacks were clumsy, coupled with many points lost, giving the other side the momentum to attack, and they were unable to display their strengths. In the second set, Wang and Zheng seemed to see the light after a storm and cheered up. Their momentum was strong and coordinated with each other, leaving the opponent no chance to attack. They won six consecutive games and won 6-0, which was commendable. Thus, the battle of the third set became a matter of life and death. Both sides worked hard and did not give way to each other. The scores fluctuated up and down, and the spectators were also engrossed. Wang and Zheng continued to work hard and eventually won 7-5, creating a score of 2-1.

Italy and Japan each win one match

(Dentsu, Geneva, 11th) The Davis Cup tennis European group final between Japan and Italy began today. The results of the first day's singles matches are as follows:

(Japan) Harada 6-4, 6-3, 7-5 vs. De Morpurgo (Italy)

(Right) Otakura (big) of Meiji (Left) Lin Baohua of China (photographed by Mo Tianxiang)

Important News

Record of the First Annual Meeting of the China Children's Education Society (2) 89

Discussions on the Boat

The situation of the first annual meeting of the China Children's Education Society held in Wuxi has been reported in detail in this newspaper for the past two days. Yesterday (11th), the meeting continued. The reception office pre-hired a large boat, towed by a steamboat. They departed from the Taihu Lake area at 9 AM. Various proposals were discussed on the boat. At noon, they arrived at the Garden of Five Mile Lake. After sightseeing, they returned to the boat for lunch. They toured Turtle Head Isle at 2 PM and continued discussions on the boat at 3 PM. They returned to the Railway Hotel at 6 PM. The various proposals discussed are listed below:

Resolutions Passed 90

Chairman Li Qingsong announced the opening of the meeting for discussion, as follows: (1) Proposal on whether to stipulate concrete graduation standards for kindergartens, proposed by Chen Heqin. It was resolved to organize a Kindergarten Experimental Research Committee to preside over the handling of experimental liaison matters. The experimental work will be carried out by members of the Society. Five members were elected, and the results were Chen Heqin, Zhang Zonglin, Ge Liting, Hu Shuyi, and Xia Chengfeng. Chen Heqin was responsible for convening the meeting. (2) Proposal on whether to stipulate concrete daily schedules for kindergartens, proposed by Chen Heqin. It was resolved to merge it with the previous proposal and be responsible for the research by the committee. It was also resolved to request Mr. Chen Heqin to appoint two people to join the work. Xu Shibi and Tu Zhemei were immediately appointed. (3) Proposal on special education through social experiments by specially appointed organizations of the Society, proposed by Xizhong Experimental Primary School. It was resolved that specially appointed organizations and members could hold it when necessary. (4) Proposal that the Society select and collect children's education achievements from various organizations and members every year to hold a children's education exhibition at a suitable location for mutual learning, proposed by Chen Heqin. It was resolved to pass the original proposal, which will be handled by the Executive Committee of the Society for the time being. (5) Proposal to hold a recreational competition once a year or every semester to improve educational achievements and increase research interest, proposed by Chen Heqin. It was resolved to hold it once a year. (6) Proposal on how to stipulate concrete methods for contacting children's families, proposed by Chen Jianheng. It was resolved to change it to a study on how to contact and improve children's families, and the Executive Committee will appoint members from among the members to form a committee. (7) Proposal to request the Society to add an introduction and agency department for children's education books and supplies, proposed by Shen Shanzhi and Ge Chengxun. It was resolved to hand it over to the Executive Committee for handling. (8) Proposal to organize a children's education hall or library, proposed by Jin Xiaoxian. (9) Proposal on how to organize a scientific and artistic children's library to cultivate children's self-learning ability, proposed by Zhao Keshi, Lu Zhuiping, and Zhu Junsheng. It was resolved that the above two proposals would be merged for discussion, and the original proposal would be revised to (Promote and experiment with children's libraries) and handed over to the Executive Committee for handling. The methods are as follows: A. Solicit planning and sorting reports from various schools. B. Agree to organize an ideal library on their own in each school and report the results in the next session. C. Submit a request to the Ministry of Education to order the education administrative agencies of all provinces and cities to establish and promote it. (10) The Children's Education Magazine should be published on time, proposed by Shen Shanzhi and Ge Chengxun. It was resolved to ask the Executive Committee to pay attention. (11) The manuscript published in Children's Education should be given considerable royalties to the original author when editing a series of books, proposed by Jin Xiaoxian. It was resolved to organize a publishing committee to handle it. (12) How to implement children's music education, proposed by Lu Jingyi. It was resolved that the next Executive Committee would hire experts to form a committee to study children's music education. (13) Increase a large number of members, proposed by Zhang Zonglin. It was resolved that the Executive Committee would handle all introduction and review matters. (14) The proposal to introduce Yangzhong Experimental Primary School to join the Society as a group member was approved by Ma Ketan. It was resolved to pass it. (15) Can members of the Society in various places have a considerable organization for liaison, proposed by Chen Jianheng? (16) Proposal to add a correspondence research department, proposed by Xizhong Experimental Primary School. It was resolved to merge the above two proposals for discussion (correspondence research) methods. (17) The central question for the next conference. It was resolved to still use (Children's Center Education) as the central question for the next conference. (18) Although the central question of the conference has been determined, can several specialized questions be slightly compiled during the discussion of the question? It was resolved to reject it. (19) Organize a preparatory annual meeting committee, proposed by Dong Jiejian. It was resolved to hire seven members as members to preside over all community affairs of the annual meeting. (20) The date of the next conference. It was resolved to hold it in the spring of next year. (21) The location of the next conference. It was resolved to select Suzhou and Shanghai and let the Executive Committee choose one of them. (22) The next exhibition of achievements. It was resolved that the next conference would hold (Children's Art Exhibition). (23) The next conference will hold a children's recreational performance. It was resolved to deny it.

Mr. Chen's Speech

Mr. Chen Heqin told this newspaper's reporter this morning (11th) that the most important discussion proposal of this annual meeting is (Children's Center Education Experimental Research) and (Experimenting with the Ministry's Provisional Kindergarten and Primary School Curriculum Standards). Children's Center Education is the latest overall non-divisional education method that should meet the needs of society and be suitable for children's lives as the foundation. The Children's Center Education Special Issue of the magazine issued by the Society was issued and brought yesterday, all about the theory, theory, and application methods, etc. At the meeting yesterday (10th), the following two research associations were specially generated for experiments: (1) Ministry-leaning curriculum experiment research committee: Gulou Kindergarten, Nanjing Xiqu Experimental Primary School, Xiaozhuang Experimental School, Nanjing Girls' High School Experimental Primary School, Nanzhong Experimental Primary School, Zhongda Experimental School, Nanjing Central District Experimental Primary School, Suzhong Experimental Primary School, Tongzhong Experimental Primary School, Taizhong Experimental Primary School. (2) Children's Center Education Experimental Research Association. Ge Liting, Chen Heqin, Zhang Zonglin, Dong Renjian, and Hu Shuyi were elected as members. Gong Jiaji and Ma Ke were proposed as alternate members.

Opening a Memorial Service

Ms. He Yuxiu, a member of the newspaper's executive committee, graduated from the Education Institute of Zhongda University and served as the director of Nanjing Gulou Kindergarten for two years. On the first day of this month, she contracted a contagious disease while taking care of her brother who was suffering from severe typhoid fever and died in Beijing at the age of only twenty-six. Last night, the Society held a meeting and presented wreaths at the Railway Hotel. Chairman Chen Heqin presided over the meeting, followed by Ma Da, a representative of the family, who reported the circumstances before her death. Many members temporarily donated elegiac couplets.

Lin Baohua and Qiu Feihai of China versus Matsuo and Sagara of Meiji

The situation during the doubles match (photographed by Wang Kai)

Important Talk by the Supervisor of Students Studying in Japan 91

Determining the Direction of Studying Abroad

Improving the Method of Supplementary Subsidy Geng Fund

Mr. Wang KeRen, supervisor of students studying in Japan, returned to China on official business the other day. The reporter met him on the way, and went to his residence. In addition to greetings, there were also important talks on education. The following is a brief description: Studying in Japan is near and costs less. There are many people who go there, so the supervisors have difficulty dealing with matters because the supervisors are of various qualities. The busiest months for the supervisor's office are March, April, May, June, September, because the Japanese semester starts in April and the graduation of each school ends in March. Therefore, there are many things to do in March and April, such as introducing admission and supplementary subsidies. The method of supplementary subsidy Geng Fund is not only considered bad by the Chinese, but also felt inappropriate by the Japanese. It is necessary to amend it. At 7 AM today (11th), a meeting was held with the vice minister, the director of higher education, the section chief, and the directors and counselors of each department of the Ministry of Education. It has been decided that, in accordance with the recent policy of the National Government to abolish the Sino-Japanese Cultural Convention, the supplementary subsidy Geng Fund will be re-established and submitted to the National Government for approval. It will also be requested that the Ministry of Education improve the method of issuing certificates to students studying in Japan, so as to remedy the situation. The Ministry of Education also intends to formulate a principle for students studying abroad as a whole, to determine the direction of studying abroad, such as the examination of the qualifications of students studying in Japan, the assessment of academic performance, and the management system for the allocation of funds, etc.

The Ministry Orders All Schools to Set Up More Free Places 92

To Accommodate Children of Workers

The Secretariat of the Central Executive Committee previously sent a letter to the Ministry of Education requesting the Jiangsu Provincial Consolidation Committee to instruct public and private schools in various provinces to give priority to accommodating children of workers. The Ministry of Education had previously ordered all schools to set up more free places, which already contained this meaning. It has recently replied that the letter from your office was approved by the Standing Committee and submitted to the Jiangsu Provincial Party Affairs Consolidation Committee, which forwarded the Xixian Consolidation Committee to request that the order be issued to public schools in various provinces to provide free places and give priority to admitting children of workers. The Ministry has been submitted to the Ministry of Education for approval. It has been copied and forwarded to your office for your reference, and a copy of the original letter has been sent to the Ministry. The Ministry has issued an instruction numbered 13000, requiring schools at all levels to set up more free places, stating that poor children in the school may be exempted from some or all of the fees that should be paid. The plan to improve national education and the plan to improve elementary education also stipulate that kindergartens and nurseries should not charge tuition fees in principle, and those that charge fees should still set up more free places for poor students. The so-called poor children and poor students already include children of workers. As for the admission of students, the children of workers and farmers should be given priority, and a detailed method should be established and implemented on a global basis. This should be replied accordingly. Please refer to the original letter for your reference.

One Year of Tropical Disease Research 93

Hong Shilu of the Tropical Disease Research Institute has concluded his 18th year. He has submitted four types of work overview and research publications for the year, (1) Various nematodes in the intestines of Xiaoshan (Hong Shilu), (2) A new identification method for Mimosa (Huang Ming), (3) One method of preparing transparent specimens of Megalodiscus (Ke Tu), (4) Detection of a parasite similar to Theileria Farra in human red blood cells, to the Ministry of Education. The Ministry of Education appreciated his research findings.

Beijing Municipal Education Bureau

Restricting Private Middle Schools from Enrolling Female Students 94

Special Equipment Should Be Available for the Management of Female Students

(Central News Agency) The Beijing Municipal Education Bureau believes that private middle schools in the city are seeking to expand the number of students and are enrolling mixed male and female students. They are disregarding the various facilities that should be available for the enrollment of female students, resulting in many obstacles in school management and student life. According to educational principles and the principle of equality between men and women, co-education is of course desirable, but without appropriate facilities, there are often many malpractices. The Bureau yesterday specially instructed all private middle schools that, unless there are special facilities, they will stop enrolling female students from the 19th year. If it is necessary to enroll female students, they must first submit an application to the Bureau for approval before they can do so. Otherwise, once discovered, they will be severely punished.

Municipal Training Department Announces Results of Party Education Inspection in the City 95

14 Schools Should Be Encouraged, 41 Schools Should Be Corrected

A Total of 4 Schools Should Be Warned, Statistics for Elementary Schools Are Still Being Compiled

(National News Agency) In this city, many schools earnestly implement party ideology education, but not a few are perfunctory. The Municipal Training Department believes that party ideology education is of great importance. Without strict assessment and effective guidance, it is not enough to eliminate its malpractices and promote its progress. After two years of efforts and one or two inspections, initial results have become visible. However, the number of schools in the city, both public and private, is so large that statistics are already difficult, and inspections are even more difficult to carry out thoroughly. Therefore, during the last municipal training meeting, it was decided to proceed by district. Elementary schools would be inspected by each district and their fourth-grade students tested for comparison. Secondary schools would be inspected by the Municipal Training Department for dedicated responsibility. The details were previously reported in this newspaper. Now, inspections of both elementary and secondary schools have been completed. A total of 59 secondary schools were inspected (statistics for elementary schools are still being compiled). The achievements, both good and bad, have been carefully reviewed and graded. Schools that performed better were given encouragement, while those that performed poorly were given warnings, and the Bureau of Education was notified to handle them separately. There were also many schools where the second performance was poor but the third was remarkably improved. The effectiveness of the inspections can be seen from the following record of the third inspection results regarding secondary schools:

The following 14 schools should be encouraged: Chengzhong Middle School, Jianguo Middle School, Junyi Middle School, Guangzhao Middle School, Wusong Middle School, Huahua Middle School, Yucai Middle School, Qingnian Middle School, Wuben Girls' School, Jingye Middle School, Minli Middle School, Sanyu Middle School, Xinmin Middle School, Nanyang Middle School.

The following 41 schools should be corrected: Fudan Middle School, Guanghua Affiliated Middle School, Qinghua Middle School, Minzhi Girls' Middle School, Minzhi Middle School, Shenfan Girls' Middle School, Qingxin Middle School, Chizhi Affiliated Middle School, Daxia Affiliated Middle School, Peiming Girls' Middle School, Nanyang Girls' Middle School, Qingxin Girls' Middle School, Shanghai Elementary and Middle School, Dongwu Second Middle School, Dahua Middle School, Minli Girls' Middle School, Southeast Women's Sports School, Huizhong Middle School, Huiling Middle School, Zhonghua Vocational School, Pudong Middle School, YMCA Middle School, Huizhong Girls' Middle School, Fudan Shizhong, Renhe Obstetrics Patriotic Girls' Middle School, Nanyang Model Middle School, Danhua Middle School, Rural Normal Wuxing Middle School, Zhengfeng Middle School, Huzhou Travelers in Shanghai Middle School, Liangjiang Women's Sports, Meilun Middle School, Shanghai Middle School, Shangde Middle School, Zhende Girls' Middle School, Zhaoji Middle School, Biwen Girls' Middle School, Qinye Girls' Middle School, China Women's Sports.

The following 4 schools should be warned: Yanmaoshi Girls' School, Muertang Girls' School, Zhongxi Girls' School, Jinglin Middle School.

County Education Bureau Focuses on Promoting Phonetic Symbols 96

This Year, It Plans to Redistribute Locations for Civilian Schools

The Shanghai County Education Bureau believes that phonetic symbols are the foundation of literacy, and the development of social education depends on them. It has decided to add symbol instruction in all civilian schools this year and gradually find ways to promote them for universal adoption. It also plans to redistribute the locations of civilian schools based on the situation in each district. All distribution and promotion methods will be planned and implemented by the Civilian Education Committee.

Food Relief and Savings Methods 98

Joint Proposal by the Departments of Civil Affairs and Agriculture

County Government Ordered to Implement

The Shanghai County Government yesterday received instructions from the Jiangsu Department of Civil Affairs, attaching the original text of the food relief and savings methods jointly proposed by the Departments of Civil Affairs and Agriculture, ordering compliance. The original proposal is as follows: "Regarding the matter of respectfully proposing for review and approval the food relief and savings methods jointly proposed in compliance with orders: We received instructions from your government, Order No. 694, regarding how to provide relief before the new grain is harvested and how to save and store after the new grain is harvested. We were ordered to jointly draft appropriate methods and submit them for your examination and approval, etc. In compliance with this, after consultation between our departments, we respectfully submit the following methods based on our limited views: (1) Relief methods before the new grain is harvested: The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce and the Rice Industry Association should raise large sums of money to purchase large quantities of foreign rice to be transported to various counties in the interior for continuous supply. Our Department of Civil Affairs previously submitted a request to the National Chamber of Commerce to raise funds to purchase rice, and the instructions have been approved. Now, we plan to order the county magistrates to jointly handle the matter with local groups, which will be easier to organize. (2) Issue a general order to all counties to allocate some of their stored grain to purchase rice in Shanghai and set up bureaus to sell it at a fair price. If the grain funds are insufficient, encourage local gentry and merchants to contribute to the funding, and ensure that it is implemented as soon as possible. Our Department of Civil Affairs has also applied for this, and upon approval, we will order compliance. As for strictly prohibiting exports from the province, preventing smuggling, and cracking down on unscrupulous merchants hoarding and improper consumption, we have already issued general orders and will conduct regular inspections to avoid negligence. (3) Savings methods after the new grain is harvested: (1) Vigorously implement mandatory grain storage. The regulations of the Ministry's Grain Storage Management Committee have already been issued to all counties by our Department of Civil Affairs, and most have reported the establishment of organizations. In the future, it is not allowed to substitute grain with funds. The Department will strictly implement this and hold the Management Committee responsible. When grain prices are low, they should raise prices to buy it, and when grain prices are high, they should lower prices to sell it. All losses are allowed to be covered by deducting a certain amount from the funds collected. If this is done, the grain price can be maintained at a balance, preventing unscrupulous merchants from monopolizing it. Promote credit cooperatives to use stored grain as collateral for loans, so that farmers' capital can circulate and food can still be stored. Hold the Grain Storage Management Committee responsible, and consult with the district chiefs to plan carefully and promote it together, so as to achieve results and gain practical benefits. The above proposed sections are the same opinions after consultation between our departments. We respectfully submit them in compliance with the order, and request your review and approval."

Airmail Service at Shanghai Post Office 99

Starting July 15th, Newspapers, etc., Can Be Mailed

It is reported that the Shanghai Postal Authority stated that starting July 15th, all kinds of newspapers, books, printed matter, and packages can be mailed via the Shanghai-Nanjing-Jiujiang-Hankou airmail route. In addition to paying the regular postage for each category (if you want to register or express mail, you will also pay the registration or express postage), regardless of the type of mail, an airmail fee of 15 cents will be added for every 20 grams. However, packages mailed in Shanghai must still be inspected by the Shanghai Customs Inspection Office stationed at the Postal Administration before they can be accepted for mailing.

The Two-Percent Donation in the French Concession 100

Notice of Temporary Suspension of Payment

The issue of the extra two-percent donation increased by the French Concession Public Works Bureau and the Public Concession Works Department at the same time has been repeatedly raised with the French authorities by the Chinese Ratepayers Association of the French Concession, who advocated for its cancellation at the same time as the Public Concession in order to maintain credibility. A few days ago, Mr. Fould, the Director of the French Concession Public Works Bureau, invited representatives appointed by the Chinese Ratepayers Association to discuss the matter together. It is expected that it can be implemented after another meeting. Now, the Chinese Ratepayers Association, fearing that citizens do not understand the negotiation situation and that conflicts may occur due to the collection of donations, has issued another notice to inform the public. The notice is as follows: "Regarding the matter of the French Concession Public Works Bureau increasing the extra two-percent donation at the same time as the Public Concession Works Department in the 16th year, our association has repeatedly raised the matter with the French authorities, advocating for its cancellation at the same time as the Public Concession in order to maintain credibility. Later, Mr. Fould, the Director of the French Concession Public Works Bureau, invited our association to appoint representatives to visit the bureau on the 11th to discuss the matter together. We went as scheduled and, after a long discussion, Mr. Fould agreed. It is expected that it can be implemented after further consultations. However, in the past few days, citizens in the concession have repeatedly inquired about the results of the negotiations and whether or not to pay the 12 percent donation. As this matter is currently in the negotiation period, payment should be temporarily suspended to avoid misunderstandings. We will issue another notice to pay after a decision is made."

The French Business Water and Electricity Strike 101

Mediation Failed Again Yesterday

The French business water and electricity strike has been going on for many days and has not yet been resolved. Here is a record of the situation yesterday:

The general meeting resolved important cases. More than 600 workers gathered at the Public Stadium yesterday afternoon at 3:00 p.m. The Municipal Party Department sent Xu Yefu to attend and provide guidance. The Public Security Bureau's Second District ordered the police to protect the meeting. Chairman Chen Puai reported that the tramcars of the factory had been damaged by attacks in recent days, and today it was reported that the water pipes had been destroyed. The factory was quite panicked. The Municipal Party Department has convened a party, government, and military meeting, and there are concrete methods for the strike, which can be easily resolved soon. I hope that all workers will unite and fight to the death, and not be incited by reactionaries, leading to accidents. Then, the following was discussed: (1) Request the Municipal Party Department to transfer Chen Qiaosong's detention case to the Public Security Bureau for handling in accordance with the law. (2) Request the Municipal Party Department to convene the news media to publish the news of the labor strike of this trade union as much as possible, and ask them to uphold justice to promote the awakening of the imperialists. (3) Request the Municipal Party Department to send a letter to the Public Security Bureau prohibiting the police from protecting the French business water plant. The meeting adjourned at 5:30 p.m.

Water pipes continue to be damaged. The French business water main pipes in the west of the South Railway Station have a total of four pipes: one 32-inch pipe, one 24-inch pipe, and two 16-inch pipes. The first pipe to break was the 24-inch pipe, which was immediately repaired. Now it is learned that the 32-inch pipe has also been broken and has not yet been repaired. The 24-inch pipe broke again yesterday. The French Concession's tap water has been affected since yesterday. Users are suffering from the turbid water quality, which is not hygienic.

The Social Affairs Bureau's mediation failed. After participating in the party, government, and military meeting the day before, the Social Affairs Bureau decided to give the factory another opportunity to come to its senses, and scheduled a second mediation meeting between labor and management at 9:00 a.m. yesterday. Unexpectedly, the attitude of the capital side was still as strong as before, refusing to mediate and refusing to attend. The Social Affairs Bureau believes that the French business water and electricity company not only despises the Chinese authorities, but also remains unrepentant. All responsibilities for the future expansion of the strike should be borne by the company.

Three Cars Smashed in the French Concession Last Night 102

One Tramcar and One Trolleybus Each

Another Public Bus

One Driver Was Injured

At 8:50 p.m. last night, fifty or sixty people resembling workers gathered at the intersection of Rue Bayle and Avenue Villemon in the French Concession. A French commercial Route 22 bus, No. 213, was driving from the east. The crowd immediately took out stones and suddenly threw them at the bus. All the glass windows were completely shattered. At the same time, a French commercial Route 5 tramcar, No. 24, was smashed by dozens of people near the vegetable market on East Xinjiao Street. Driver No. 212 was seriously injured. When the police heard the alarm, they dispatched a large number of detectives to rush to the scene, but the crowd had disappeared. The injured driver and the car were sent to the police station and then to Guangci Hospital for treatment. Unexpectedly, at 10:05 p.m., a Route 18 trolleybus, No. 164, was also smashed by rocks while passing the slaughterhouse on Rue Massenet. Although detectives rushed to the scene, no one was arrested.

Domestic Matches

Ministry Order Exempting Heavy Taxes 110

The Jiangsu Provincial Match Industry Association previously submitted a request to the Ministry of Finance to exempt all taxes on matches. It is now learned that the Ministry of Finance replied to the association yesterday, saying: "We have received your letter requesting the exemption of various taxes on domestic matches. We have investigated that all domestic industrial products that have been approved to be handled in accordance with the Machine-Made Goods Tax Law are exempt from other taxes after paying taxes at the first customs station. This is the only way to give preferential treatment to domestic factories. The factories of your association members have long been treated in accordance with the above-mentioned methods and have been recorded, so there is no need to levy other taxes. As for Swedish matches, there is a situation of encroaching on Chinese matches. Our Ministry has previously drafted prevention and tax laws in order to urgently seek relief and has submitted them to the Executive Yuan for review and promulgation. There is no need to discuss the exemption of domestic match taxes requested by your association. The letter is approved for reference."

Ministry of Railways

Actively Rectifying Passenger Cars on the Beijing-Shanghai Railway 111

Minister of Railways Sun Ke recently stated that the passenger cars on the Beijing-Shanghai Railway are becoming increasingly corrupt, and passengers have many complaints, especially about the third-class seats. If this continues, it will not only affect the revenue of the railway administration but also be detrimental to the passengers. Three steps have been specifically defined to improve the situation. The first step is to send a letter to the Ministry of Military Affairs and the General Headquarters to order the troops stationed in various places that soldiers are not allowed to stretch their feet high and occupy seats on trains, so as not to hinder the safety of passengers, and to post notices in the carriages to make it universal. The second step is to strictly prohibit the sale of rotten fruits and foods on the train to emphasize hygiene, as it is the height of summer and unclean fruits and other items are often sold on the train. The third step is to strictly prohibit the road administration and train attendants from mistreating third-class passengers. If they dare to disobey, they will be severely punished once they are found out, and the general passengers are allowed to report to the stationmasters of each station if they are mistreated by the attendants. The stationmasters of each station should investigate impartially after receiving the passengers' reports and should not be biased. Violators will be severely punished.

The Shanghai-Baoshan Stamp Tax Bureau Promotes Tax Collection 112

Since Mr. Guan Jiong, Deputy Director of the Jiangsu Provincial Bureau, took over as the Director of the Shanghai-Baoshan Stamp Tax Bureau, he has worked hard to increase tax revenue. All new stages, such as the Shanghai Grand Theatre and the Guang Stage, have been affixed with stamps, and each sales agent is ordered to attend a meeting at the bureau every week to discuss sales matters and seek development. Yesterday, another notice was issued as follows: "(Regarding the notice, the stamp tax is a good tax in the world and a legitimate tax of the country. Since the stamp tax regulations were promulgated, after silently observing the social situation, it has been many years, and habits have gradually been formed. Recently, merchants and people know that the stamp tax has the effect of protecting legal rights. On the one hand, they fulfill the obligation of paying taxes to the country, and on the other hand, they enjoy the right to be protected by the people. Therefore, they are happy to purchase and affix stamps and actively implement them, and tax revenue has increased compared to before. The location is indeed in the central area of the commercial port, and the personnel are busy and the people are enlightened. It is indeed the crown of all places. The people respect national taxes and have sympathy. Since the Director of this Bureau took office, the examination of files and the audit of tax collection and sales have indeed been promoted more than before, but the cities and villages are vast, and the persuasion may not be thorough. Now, we are ordered to urge and tighten the collection, and we have to strive for progress. In addition to ordering the sales agents in the north and south cities to comply, we hereby earnestly notify the merchants and people to know that the ledgers and vouchers have been affixed with stamps in accordance with the regulations, and those that have not been checked or have not been affixed with the full amount should be checked and re-affixed. As for the delivery notes and money receipts, etc., they are the important vouchers for business transactions. Now, all places in Ning and Su have implemented compliance and affixed stamps, and the inspection is very strict. The shops in this port must pay attention to affixing stamps to the aforementioned documents and do not neglect to miss them. It is the responsibility of this Bureau to send personnel to investigate regularly. If tax-evading documents are found, they will only be punished in accordance with the law and cannot be leniently forgiven. Each inspector wears a badge when performing official duties and is given a license with a photo attached. The licenses of the inspectors dispatched by the previous Director have been recovered and canceled. Now, this Director has selected and dispatched inspectors and has re-manufactured licenses for application. In the future, merchants and people must affix stamps to all vouchers in accordance with the regulations and must not violate or omit them, so as not to interfere with the investigation and punishment. Special notice is hereby given on July 3rd, 19th year of the Republic of China, Guan Jiong, Deputy Director of the Jiangsu Provincial Stamp Tax Bureau and Director of the Shanghai-Baoshan Stamp Tax Bureau."

The Ratepayers Association Sends a Letter to the Public Works Department for Rectification

The house donation collected by the Public Works Department has always been calculated according to the house rent on the lease. Unexpectedly, this time, when collecting the house donation for the autumn of this year, No. 180 was not calculated according to the house rent of 143 yuan per month, but was increased to 300 yuan per month using the valuation method. Shanghai Shipping Business

Page 14

The Success of Joint Operation 118

Effective Trial Operation on All Routes of Zhejiang Sea

The Shanghai-Taiwan route, historically operated by four companies, saw the addition of two new companies last year. This led to intense competition among the six companies in passenger and freight services. Fares and rates were drastically reduced, making it unsustainable to cover expenses. After incurring significant losses, representatives from the Ministry of Transportation came to Shanghai and, through repeated mediation, a new method of joint operation was agreed upon this year. The six companies, Chuanshan, Daxing, Taizhou, Zhoushan, Ping'an, etc., established a joint office in the southern part of Shanghai. Each company sent a staff member to manage affairs at a designated desk. In terms of operation, revenue and expenses were combined for the six ships. The method of mutual dispatch of personnel for supervision was adopted to demonstrate impartiality, and all ticket prices and freight rates were publicly set, prohibiting private increases or decreases. Since the six companies began cooperating, operations have been normal, and revenues have greatly increased. The joint operation of the six companies' ships on the Shanghai-Taiwan route is based on the total annual revenue of 800,000 yuan from both passenger and freight services. The largest ship is allocated 135,000 yuan per year, while the smallest is allocated 120,000 yuan. Any subsequent surpluses or deficits are distributed or covered accordingly. Since the joint operation began half a year ago, the companies have jointly examined the business and found that it has exceeded expectations. Compared to the previous period when each company operated independently, revenue has increased by 40 percent. It is expected that by the end of the year, revenue will exceed one million yuan, breaking the operational record for the Shanghai-Taiwan route.

On the Shanghai-Ningbo route, this year China Merchants, Sanbei, Ningshao, and Taikoo, in order to increase freight rates and eliminate price reductions resulting from mutual competition, after consultation between Yu Qiaqing and various shipping companies, also adopted a division of labor and cooperation system. The four companies implemented joint operation. The method involved listing the annual revenue from passenger and freight services between Shanghai and Ningbo as a standard, and determining the share each ship should receive based on its usual business and tonnage. Ningshao's Xin Ningshao was ranked first, Sanbei's Xin Ningxing was ranked second, followed by Xin Jiangtian and Xin Beijing. The highest annual amount was 230,000 yuan, and the lowest was 180,000 to 190,000 yuan. Daily export and import cargo manifests were shared among the four companies for review. For the past half-year, the four companies' business, both passenger and freight, has exceeded the set amount, increasing by at least 20 percent compared to the past. The reason for this is that the practice of excessive commissions has been eliminated, and all proceeds go to the public.

On the Tongyang route, competition between Dada and Datong of this port on the Tongyang route this year has been intense. Datong has also built new ships, and both sides have exerted all their efforts to compete. Yesterday, Dada Company's Dahe Wheel and Datong Company's Longhe Wheel were ordered to temporarily suspend operations. The two ships were each ordered to load more than ten days' worth of coal and were scheduled to sail to the upper reaches of the Yangtze River this morning, where they would await deployment in Changyue. Outbound voyages from Shanghai to Tongyang will be reduced by two trips per week for the time being.

The Customs Needs Land in Southern Shanghai 119

Correspondence Between the Public Works Bureau and the Dredging Bureau

The area along the Jiangnan riverside in the Nanshi Sixteenth Pier, such as the Cuifeng Wharf and Xuejia浜, is an area of land that had been leased from the Dredging Bureau by the timber trade guild and the bamboo trade association. Subsequently, due to the needs of the Public Works and Patrol Bureau, the timber trade guild subleased the land. This arrangement continued after the Municipal Government's Public Works Bureau took over. Recently, it was reported that the Jianghai Customs requires the aforementioned land along the river in Nanshi to inspect goods and operate offices. Therefore, they requested to lease the land from the Dredging Bureau. The Dredging Bureau replied that since the land is currently being subleased to the Public Works Bureau, it has sent a letter to the Public Works Bureau proposing to reclaim the land for its own use. The Public Works Bureau, after receiving the letter, replied that it is still uncertain whether this land exists given the new routes and coastline recently determined in the city. Therefore, it has prepared the latest map and sent it to the Dredging Bureau for review.

The Ordnance Factory Will Tomorrow 122

Distribute Compensation to Bereaved Workers 123

Following the accident in the medicine filling room of the 63rd Ordnance Factory, the factory staff organized a post-disaster committee for the bereaved families, initiated fundraising, and submitted a request to the Ministry of Military and Political Affairs for compensation. An order has now been received for a compensation of 300 yuan per person. In addition to the 120 yuan for the coffin and burial expenses paid last time, the factory staff has collectively donated over 8,400 yuan. After the committee completed its investigation into the circumstances of the families of the deceased and injured workers, it was found that there were 23 deaths and 26 injuries. It is reported that the committee will distribute the funds separately at 2:00 PM tomorrow in the factory's main hall, with Executive Committee members Xu Mujun and others supervising the count. Each of the deceased will receive a compensation of 300 yuan, except for foreman Shi Changhua, who, due to his long years of service in the factory, will receive a separate compensation of 800 yuan. The remaining injured workers will each receive between 30 and 50 yuan, depending on the severity of their injuries.

Shanghai Bank

Begins Using Armored Cars to Transport Silver 131

No Different from American Silver Delivery Vehicles

In view of the recent dangers in transporting cash, the Shanghai Commercial & Savings Bank, as a precautionary measure, ordered two armored locomotives from the local American Tong Company, modeled after the latest silver delivery vehicles in New York and Chicago. They have now been completed and will be put into use immediately. The entire vehicle is painted fish-white, and the paint shines brightly. The driver's and passengers' seats are protected by iron plates on both sides and in front. When the vehicle stops, the rear can be removed as a seating area for armed guards. The police department has been requested to send personnel to escort the vehicle to prevent accidents. Outsiders do not know that it is an armored vehicle. This comprehensive equipment is for the sake of stability, making it a groundbreaking innovation in Shanghai's banking industry.

Local News 2

Headless Male Corpse Discovered on Lan Road, Yangshupu 133

The Deceased Is Not Yet Identified

Yesterday morning, an unidentified headless male corpse was found in an open space in the middle section of Lan Road, Yangshupu, Pudong, Shanghai. Nearby residents rushed to watch, finding it quite bizarre. A patrolman discovered it and immediately reported it to the Yangshu police station in charge. Upon hearing the news, the police chief, considering the case to be a assassination and related to social security, immediately ordered Chinese and Western detectives to rush to investigate. The head of the male corpse had been severed, seemingly by a knife. The clothes were ordinary. Some said that the person seemed to be a nearby worker. For a time, workers from various factories went to inspect, but no one recognized him. The police have now transported the corpse to the forensic examination office on Fielun Road to await examination by the court tomorrow. Meanwhile, all detectives have been ordered to conduct a strict investigation to uncover the truth.

French National Day Tomorrow 134

There Will Be a Lantern Parade Tonight

Tomorrow is the celebration of the founding of the French Democratic Republic. The French officials, gentlemen, merchants, and scholars in Shanghai, as in previous years, are holding celebrations. The French Consul General, Mr. Gu Ganlin, has already notified the Engineering Department of the工部局 to prepare and arrange. A lantern parade will be held tonight, and a celebration will be held at the consulate tomorrow. The Engineering Department of the工部局 has sent craftsmen to erect tall pine and cypress arches in front of the French Consulate on the Bund, displaying national flags and installing colored electric lights. The reception hall is decorated with flowers and lanterns everywhere. On the lawn in front of the hall, wooden poles are placed around, with national flags and paper lanterns hanging from the top. Pine and cypress arches are also erected in front of the Customs House gate on公館馬路 and the big clock. Colored electric lights are fully installed around the big clock and on the houses. The fire brigade stations on the大自鳴鐘,新開河 and霞飛路, in addition to tying pine and cypress flower platforms with lights on the fire trucks, also hang lanterns and decorations in front of the gates. The顧家宅 Park is decorated with a wooden board city gate at the intersection of環龍路 and華龍路, fully equipped with thousands of colored electric lights. Wooden poles are placed in the alleys in the park, hanging various paper lanterns. Red and green paper lanterns are hung on the branches of large and small trees, shaped like pagodas and umbrella covers. Various paper silk models are also arranged in the pool, shaped into lifelike lanterns of birds, animals, and aquatic creatures floating on the water. Music pavilions and straw mats are also arranged to play music and show movies to entertain guests in the evening. In addition, the French patrol station has floats, warships, birds, aquatic animals, and other unique lanterns, ready to participate in the lantern parade competition tonight. The French patrol station will ensure that the roads are crowded with tourists at that time, so the French General Inspector Fu Yu ordered each patrol station to send Chinese, Western, and Yue detectives to take care of the areas through which the lantern parade passes.
